const fs = require(&apos;fs&apos;);
const zlib = require(&apos;zlib&apos;);

const server = http.createServer((req, res) =&gt; {
  const filename = req.headers.filename;
  console.log(&apos;File request received: &apos; + filename);
  req
    .pipe(zlib.createGunzip())
    .pipe(fs.createWriteStream(filename))
    .on(&apos;finish&apos;, () =&gt; {
      res.writeHead(201, {
        &apos;Content-Type&apos;: &apos;text/plain&apos;
      });
      res.end(&apos;That\&apos;s it\n&apos;);
      console.log(`File saved: ${filename}`);
    });
});

const fs = require(&apos;fs&apos;);
const zlib = require(&apos;zlib&apos;);
const crypto = require(&apos;crypto&apos;);

const server = http.createServer((req, res) =&gt; {
  const filename = req.headers.filename;
  console.log(&apos;File request received: &apos; + filename);
  req
    .pipe(crypto.createDecipher(&apos;aes192&apos;, &apos;a_shared_secret&apos;))
    .pipe(zlib.createGunzip())
    .pipe(fs.createWriteStream(filename))
    .on(&apos;finish&apos;, () =&gt; {
      res.writeHead(201, {
        &apos;Content-Type&apos;: &apos;text/plain&apos;
      });
      res.end(&apos;That\&apos;s it\n&apos;);
      console.log(`File saved: ${filename}`);
    });
});

  }
}

&#x4F46;&#x662F;&#xFF0C;&#x8FD9;&#x5BF9;&#x4E8E;stream&#x5B9E;&#x73B0;&#x8005;&#x6765;&#x8BF4;&#x662F;&#x4E00;&#x4E2A;&#x7279;&#x5B9A;&#x7684;&#x95EE;&#x9898;&#xFF0C;&#x6240;&#x4EE5;&#x6211;&#x4EEC;&#x5C06;&#x4E0D;&#x7ECF;&#x5E38;&#x5904;&#x7406;&#x5B83;&#x3002;</blockquote><p>&#x6211;&#x4EEC;&#x53EF;&#x4EE5;&#x901A;&#x8FC7;&#x4FEE;&#x6539;&#x4E4B;&#x524D;&#x521B;&#x5EFA;&#x7684;<code>entropyServer</code>&#x6A21;&#x5757;&#x6765;&#x6F14;&#x793A;&#x53EF;&#x5199;&#x5165;&#x7684;<code>stream</code>&#x7684;<code>back-pressure</code>&#xFF1A;</p><div class="widget-codetool" style="display:none"><div class="widget-codetool--inner"><span class="selectCode code-tool" data-toggle="tooltip" data-placement="top" title="" data-original-title="&#x5168;&#x9009;"></span> <span type="button" class="copyCode code-tool" data-toggle="tooltip" data-placement="top" data-clipboard-text="const Chance = require(&apos;chance&apos;);
const chance = new Chance();

require(&apos;http&apos;).createServer((req, res) =&gt; {
  res.writeHead(200, {
    &apos;Content-Type&apos;: &apos;text/plain&apos;
  });

  function generateMore() { //[1]
    while (chance.bool({
        likelihood: 95
      })) {
      const shouldContinue = res.write(
        chance.string({
          length: (16 * 1024) - 1
        }) //[2]
      );
      if (!shouldContinue) { //[3]
        console.log(&apos;Backpressure&apos;);
        return res.once(&apos;drain&apos;, generateMore);
      }
    }
    res.end(&apos;\nThe end...\n&apos;, () =&gt; console.log(&apos;All data was sent&apos;));
  }
  generateMore();
}).listen(8080, () =&gt; console.log(&apos;Listening on http://localhost:8080&apos;));" title="" data-original-title="&#x590D;&#x5236;"></span> <span type="button" class="saveToNote code-tool" data-toggle="tooltip" data-placement="top" title="" data-original-title="&#x653E;&#x8FDB;&#x7B14;&#x8BB0;"></span></div></div><pre class="javascript hljs"><code class="javascript"><span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> Chance = <span class="hljs-built_in">require</span>(<span class="hljs-string">&apos;chance&apos;</span>);

  });

  <span class="hljs-function"><span class="hljs-keyword">function</span> <span class="hljs-title">generateMore</span>(<span class="hljs-params"></span>) </span>{ <span class="hljs-comment">//[1]</span>
    <span class="hljs-keyword">while</span> (chance.bool({
        <span class="hljs-attr">likelihood</span>: <span class="hljs-number">95</span>

      <span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> shouldContinue = res.write(

          <span class="hljs-attr">length</span>: (<span class="hljs-number">16</span> * <span class="hljs-number">1024</span>) - <span class="hljs-number">1</span>

      );
      <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (!shouldContinue) { <span class="hljs-comment">//[3]</span>

  }
  generateMore();
}).listen(<span class="hljs-number">8080</span>, () =&gt; <span class="hljs-built_in">console</span>.log(<span class="hljs-string">&apos;Listening on const fs = require(&apos;fs&apos;);
const path = require(&apos;path&apos;);
const mkdirp = require(&apos;mkdirp&apos;);

class ToFileStream extends stream.Writable {
  constructor() {
    super({
      objectMode: true
    });
  }

  _write(chunk, encoding, callback) {
    mkdirp(path.dirname(chunk.path), err =&gt; {
      if (err) {
        return callback(err);
      }
      fs.writeFile(chunk.path, chunk.content, callback);
    });
  }
}

data-placement="top" data-clipboard-text="const stream = require(&apos;stream&apos;);
const util = require(&apos;util&apos;);

class ReplaceStream extends stream.Transform {
  constructor(searchString, replaceString) {
    super();
    this.searchString = searchString;
    this.replaceString = replaceString;
    this.tailPiece = &apos;&apos;;
  }

  _transform(chunk, encoding, callback) {
    const pieces = (this.tailPiece + chunk)         //[1]
      .split(this.searchString);
    const lastPiece = pieces[pieces.length - 1];
    const tailPieceLen = this.searchString.length - 1;

    this.tailPiece = lastPiece.slice(-tailPieceLen);     //[2]
    pieces[pieces.length - 1] = lastPiece.slice(0,-tailPieceLen);

    this.push(pieces.join(this.replaceString));       //[3]
    callback();
  }

  _flush(callback) {
    this.push(this.tailPiece);
    callback();
  }
}

  fromArray.obj(files)             //[1]

class ParallelStream extends stream.Transform {
  constructor(userTransform) {
    super({objectMode: true});
    this.userTransform = userTransform;
    this.running = 0;
    this.terminateCallback = null;
  }

  _transform(chunk, enc, done) {
    this.running++;
    this.userTransform(chunk, enc, this._onComplete.bind(this), this.push.bind(this));
    done();
  }

  _flush(done) {
    if(this.running &gt; 0) {
      this.terminateCallback = done;
    } else {
      done();
    }
  }

  _onComplete(err) {
    this.running--;
    if(err) {
      return this.emit(&apos;error&apos;, err);
    }
    if(this.running === 0) {
      this.terminateCallback &amp;&amp; this.terminateCallback();
    }
  }
}

module.exports = ParallelStream;" title="" data-original-title="&#x590D;&#x5236;"></span> <span type="button" class="saveToNote code-tool" data-toggle="tooltip" data-placement="top" title="" data-original-title="&#x653E;&#x8FDB;&#x7B14;&#x8BB0;"></span></div></div><pre class="javascript hljs"><code class="javascript"><span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> stream = <span class="hljs-built_in">require</span>(<span class="hljs-string">&apos;stream&apos;</span>);

<span class="hljs-class"><span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title">ParallelStream</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">extends</span> <span class="hljs-title">stream</span>.<span class="hljs-title">Transform</span> </span>{
  <span class="hljs-keyword">constructor</span>(userTransform) {
    <span class="hljs-keyword">super</span>({<span class="hljs-attr">objectMode</span>: <span class="hljs-literal">true</span>});
    <span class="hljs-keyword">this</span>.userTransform = userTransform;
    <span class="hljs-keyword">this</span>.running = <span class="hljs-number">0</span>;
    <span class="hljs-keyword">this</span>.terminateCallback = <span class="hljs-literal">null</span>;
  }

  _transform(chunk, enc, done) {
    <span class="hljs-keyword">this</span>.running++;
    <span class="hljs-keyword">this</span>.userTransform(chunk, enc, <span class="hljs-keyword">this</span>._onComplete.bind(<span class="hljs-keyword">this</span>), <span class="hljs-keyword">this</span>.push.bind(<span class="hljs-keyword">this</span>));
    done();
  }

  _flush(done) {
    <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span>(<span class="hljs-keyword">this</span>.running &gt; <span class="hljs-number">0</span>) {
      <span class="hljs-keyword">this</span>.terminateCallback = done;
    } <span class="hljs-keyword">else</span> {
      done();
    }
  }

  _onComplete(err) {
    <span class="hljs-keyword">this</span>.running--;
    <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span>(err) {
      <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">this</span>.emit(<span class="hljs-string">&apos;error&apos;</span>, err);
    }
    <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span>(<span class="hljs-keyword">this</span>.running === <span class="hljs-number">0</span>) {
      <span class="hljs-keyword">this</span>.terminateCallback &amp;&amp; <span class="hljs-keyword">this</span>.terminateCallback();
    }
  }
}

<span class="hljs-built_in">module</span>.exports = ParallelStream;</code></pre><p>&#x6211;&#x4EEC;&#x6765;&#x5206;&#x6790;&#x4E00;&#x4E0B;&#x8FD9;&#x4E2A;&#x65B0;&#x7684;&#x81EA;&#x5B9A;&#x4E49;&#x7684;&#x7C7B;&#x3002;&#x6B63;&#x5982;&#x4F60;&#x6240;&#x770B;&#x5230;&#x7684;&#x4E00;&#x6837;&#xFF0C;&#x6784;&#x9020;&#x51FD;&#x6570;&#x63A5;&#x53D7;&#x4E00;&#x4E2A;<code>userTransform()</code>&#x51FD;&#x6570;&#x4F5C;&#x4E3A;&#x53C2;&#x6570;&#xFF0C;&#x7136;&#x540E;&#x5C06;&#x5176;&#x53E6;&#x5B58;&#x4E3A;&#x4E00;&#x4E2A;&#x5B9E;&#x4F8B;&#x53D8;&#x91CF;&#xFF1B;&#x6211;&#x4EEC;&#x4E5F;&#x8C03;&#x7528;&#x7236;&#x6784;&#x9020;&#x51FD;&#x6570;&#xFF0C;&#x5E76;&#x4E14;&#x6211;&#x4EEC;&#x9ED8;&#x8BA4;&#x542F;&#x7528;&#x5BF9;&#x8C61;&#x6A21;&#x5F0F;&#x3002;</p><p>&#x63A5;&#x4E0B;&#x6765;&#xFF0C;&#x6765;&#x770B;<code>_transform()</code>&#x65B9;&#x6CD5;&#xFF0C;&#x5728;&#x8FD9;&#x4E2A;&#x65B9;&#x6CD5;&#x4E2D;&#xFF0C;&#x6211;&#x4EEC;&#x6267;&#x884C;<code>userTransform()</code>&#x51FD;&#x6570;&#xFF0C;&#x7136;&#x540E;&#x589E;&#x52A0;&#x5F53;&#x524D;&#x6B63;&#x5728;&#x8FD0;&#x884C;&#x7684;&#x4EFB;&#x52A1;&#x4E2A;&#x6570;; &#x76F8;&#x53CD;&#xFF0C;&#x6211;&#x4EEC;&#x7ACB;&#x5373;&#x6267;&#x884C;<code>done()</code>&#x65B9;&#x6CD5;&#x3002;&#x53E6;&#x4E00;&#x65B9;&#x9762;&#xFF0C;&#x6211;&#x4EEC;&#x63D0;&#x4F9B;&#x4E86;&#x4E00;&#x4E2A;&#x7279;&#x6B8A;&#x7684;&#x56DE;&#x8C03;&#x51FD;&#x6570;&#x7ED9;<code>userTransform()</code>&#x65B9;&#x6CD5;&#xFF0C;&#x8FD9;&#x5C31;&#x662F;<code>this._onComplete()</code>&#x65B9;&#x6CD5;&#xFF1B;&#x4EE5;&#x4FBF;&#x6211;&#x4EEC;&#x5728;<code>userTransform()</code>&#x5B8C;&#x6210;&#x7684;&#x65F6;&#x5019;&#x6536;&#x5230;&#x901A;&#x77E5;&#x3002;</p><p>&#x5728;<code>Streams</code>&#x7EC8;&#x6B62;&#x4E4B;&#x524D;&#xFF0C;&#x4F1A;&#x8C03;&#x7528;<code>_flush()</code>&#x65B9;&#x6CD5;&#xFF0C;&#x6240;&#x4EE5;&#x5982;&#x679C;&#x4ECD;&#x6709;&#x4EFB;&#x52A1;&#x6B63;&#x5728;&#x8FD0;&#x884C;&#xFF0C;&#x6211;&#x4EEC;&#x53EF;&#x4EE5;&#x901A;&#x8FC7;&#x4E0D;&#x7ACB;&#x5373;&#x8C03;&#x7528;<code>done()</code>&#x56DE;&#x8C03;&#x51FD;&#x6570;&#x6765;&#x5EF6;&#x8FDF;<code>finish</code>&#x4E8B;&#x4EF6;&#x7684;&#x89E6;&#x53D1;&#x3002;&#x76F8;&#x53CD;&#xFF0C;&#x6211;&#x4EEC;&#x5C06;&#x5176;&#x5206;&#x914D;&#x7ED9;<code>this.terminateCallback</code>&#x53D8;&#x91CF;&#x3002;&#x4E3A;&#x4E86;&#x7406;&#x89E3;<code>Streams</code>&#x5982;&#x4F55;&#x6B63;&#x786E;&#x7EC8;&#x6B62;&#xFF0C;&#x6765;&#x770B;<code>_onComplete()</code>&#x65B9;&#x6CD5;&#x3002;</p><p>&#x5728;&#x6BCF;&#x7EC4;&#x5F02;&#x6B65;&#x4EFB;&#x52A1;&#x6700;&#x7EC8;&#x5B8C;&#x6210;&#x65F6;&#xFF0C;<code>_onComplete()</code>&#x65B9;&#x6CD5;&#x4F1A;&#x88AB;&#x8C03;&#x7528;&#x3002;&#x9996;&#x5148;&#xFF0C;&#x5B83;&#x4F1A;&#x68C0;&#x67E5;&#x662F;&#x5426;&#x6709;&#x4EFB;&#x52A1;&#x6B63;&#x5728;&#x8FD0;&#x884C;&#xFF0C;&#x5982;&#x679C;&#x6CA1;&#x6709;&#xFF0C;&#x5219;&#x8C03;&#x7528;<code>this.terminateCallback()</code>&#x51FD;&#x6570;&#xFF0C;&#x8FD9;&#x5C06;&#x5BFC;&#x81F4;<code>Streams</code>&#x7ED3;&#x675F;&#xFF0C;&#x89E6;&#x53D1;<code>_flush()</code>&#x65B9;&#x6CD5;&#x7684;<code>finish</code>&#x4E8B;&#x4EF6;&#x3002;</p><p>&#x5229;&#x752   this.running++;
  this.userTransform(chunk, enc,  this.push.bind(this), this._onComplete.bind(this));
  if(this.running &lt; this.concurrency) {
    done();
  } else {
    this.continueCallback = done;
  }
}" title="" data-original-title="&#x590D;&#x5236;"></span> <span type="button" class="saveToNote code-tool" data-toggle="tooltip" data-placement="top" title="" data-original-title="&#x653E;&#x8FDB;&#x7B14;&#x8BB0;"></span></div></div><pre class="javascript hljs"><code class="javascript">_transform(chunk, enc, done) {

  this.running--;
  if(err) {
    return this.emit(&apos;error&apos;, err);
  }
  const tmpCallback = this.continueCallback;
  this.continueCallback = null;
  tmpCallback &amp;&amp; tmpCallback();
  if(this.running === 0) {
    this.terminateCallback &amp;&amp; this.terminateCallback();
  }
}" title="" data-original-title="&#x590D;&#x5236;"></span> <span type="button" class="saveToNote code-tool" data-toggle="tooltip" data-placement="top" title="" data-original-title="&#x653E;&#x8FDB;&#x7B14;&#x8BB0;"></span></div></div><pre class="javascript hljs"><code class="javascript">_onComplete(err) {
  <span class="hljs-keyword">this</span>.running--;
  <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span>(err) {
    <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">this</span>.emit(<span class="hljs-string">&apos;error&apos;</span>, err);

  <span class="hljs-keyword">this</span>.continueCallback = <span class="hljs-literal">null</span>;
  tmpCallback &amp;&amp; tmpCallback();
  <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span>(<span class="hljs-keyword">this</span>.running === <span class="hljs-number">0</span>) {
    <span class="hljs-keyword">this</span>.terminateCallback &amp;&amp; <span class="hljs-keyword">this</span>.terminateCallback();
  }

code-tool" data-toggle="tooltip" data-placement="top" data-clipboard-text="const fs = require(&apos;fs&apos;);
const split = require(&apos;split&apos;);
const request = require(&apos;request&apos;);
const throughParallel = require(&apos;through2-parallel&apos;);

fs.createReadStream(process.argv[2])
  .pipe(split())
  .pipe(throughParallel.obj({concurrency: 2}, function (url, enc, done) {
    if(!url) return done();
    request.head(url, (err, response) =&gt; {
      this.push(url + &apos; is &apos; + (err ? &apos;down&apos; : &apos;up&apos;) + &apos;\n&apos;);
      done();
    });
  }))
  .pipe(fs.createWriteStream(&apos;results.txt&apos;))
  .on(&apos;finish&apos;, () =&gt; console.log(&apos;All urls were checked&apos;))

  .pipe(fs.createWriteStream(<span class="hljs-string">&apos;results.txt&apos;</span>))
  .on(<span class="hljs-string">&apos;finish&apos;</span>, () =&gt; <span class="hljs-built_in">console</span>.log(<span class="hljs-string">&apos;All urls were checked&apos;</span>))
;</code></pre><p>&#x6B63;&#x5982;&#x6211;&#x4EEC;&#x6240;&#x770B;&#x5230;&#x7684;&#xFF0C;<code>through2-parallel</code>&#x7684;&#x63A5;&#x53E3;&#x4E0E;<code>through2</code>&#x7684;&#x63A5;&#x53E3;&#x975E;&#x5E38;&#x76F8;&#x4F3C;&#xFF1B;&#x552F;&#x4E00;&#x7684;&#x4E0D;&#x540C;&#x662F;&#x5728;<code>through2-parallel</code>&#x8FD8;&#x53EF;&#x4EE5;&#x4E3A;&#x6211;&#x4EEC;&#x63D0;&#x4F9B;&#x7684;<code>transform</code>&#x51FD;&#x6570;&#x6307;&#x5B9A;&#x4E00;&#x4E2A;&#x5E76;&#x53D1;&#x9650;&#x5236;&#x3002;&#x5982;&#x679C;&#x6211;&#x4EEC;&#x5C1D;&#x8BD5;&#x8FD0;&#x884C;&#x8FD9;&#x4E2A;&#x65B0;&#x7248;&#x672C;&#x7684;<code>checkUrls</code>&#xFF0C;&#x6211;&#x4EEC;&#x4F1A;&#x770B;&#x5230;<code>results.txt</code>&#x6587;&#x4EF6;&#x5217;&#x51FA;&#x7ED3;&#x679C;&#x7684;&#x987A;&#x5E8F;&#x4E0E;&#x8F93;&#x5165;&#x6587;&#x4EF6;&#x4E2D;<br>URLs&#x7684;&#x51FA;&#x73B0;&#x987A;&#x5E8F;&#x662F;&#x4E00;&#x6837;&#x7684;&#x3002;</p><p>&#x901A;&#x8FC7;&#x8FD9;&#x4E2A;&#xFF0C;&#x6211;&#x4EEC;&#x603B;&#x7ED3;&#x4E86;&#x4F7F;&#x7528;<code>Streams</code>&#x5B9E;&#x73B0;&#x5F02;&#x6B65;&#x63A7;&#x5236;&#x6D41;&#x7684;&#x5206;&#x6790;&#xFF1B;&#x63A5;&#x4E0B;&#x6765;&#xFF0C;&#x6211;&#x4EEC;&#x7814;&#x7A76;&#x7BA1;&#x9053;&#x6A21;&#x5F0F;&#x3002;</p><h3    const fs = require(&apos;fs&apos;);
   const compressAndEncryptStream =
     require(&apos;./combinedStreams&apos;).compressAndEncrypt;
   combine(
     fs.createReadStream(process.argv[3])
     .pipe(compressAndEncryptStream(process.argv[2]))
     .pipe(fs.createWriteStream(process.argv[3] + &quot;.gz.enc&quot;))
   ).on(&apos;error&apos;, err =&gt; {
     // &#x4F7F;&#x7528;&#x7EC4;&#x5408;&#x7684;Stream&#x53EF;&#x4EE5;&#x6355;&#x83B7;&#x4EFB;&#x610F;&#x4F4D;&#x7F6E;&#x7684;&#x9519;&#x8BEF;
     console.log(err);
   });" title="" data-original-title="&#x590D;&#x5236;"></span> <span type="button" class="saveToNote code-tool" data-toggle="tooltip" data-placement="top" title="" data-original-title="&#x653E;&#x8FDB;&#x7B14;&#x8BB0;"></span></div></div><pre class="javascript hljs"><code class="javascript"><span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> combine = <span class="hljs-built_in">require</span>(<span class="hljs-string">&apos;multipipe&apos;</span>);
   <span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> fs = <span class="hljs-built_in">require</span>(<span class="hljs-string">&apos;fs&apos;</span>);
   <span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> compressAndEncryptStream =
     <span class="hljs-built_in">require</span>(<span class="hljs-string">&apos;./combinedStreams&apos;</span>).compressAndEncrypt;
   combine(
     fs.createReadStream(process.argv[<span class="hljs-number">3</span>])
     .pipe(compressAndEncryptStream(process.argv[<span class="hljs-number">2</span>]))
     .pipe(fs.createWriteStream(process.argv[<span class="hljs-number">3</span>] + <span class="hljs-string">&quot;.gz.enc&quot;</span>))
   ).on(<span class="hljs-string">&apos;error&apos;</span>, err =&gt; {
     <span class="hljs-comment">// &#x4F7F;&#x7528;&#x7EC4;&#x5408;&#x7684;Stream&#x53EF;&#x4EE5;&#x6355;&#x83B7;&#x4EFB;&#x610F;&#x4F4D;&#x7F6E;&#x7684;&#x9519;&#x8BEF;</span>

function onEnd() {
  if (++endCount === 2) {
    pack.end();
  }
}

    type: &quot;Directory&quot;,
    path: sourceA
  })
  .on(&apos;end&apos;, onEnd);

  })
  .on(&apos;end&apos;, onEnd);" title="" data-original-title="&#x590D;&#x5236;"></span> <span type="button" class="saveToNote code-tool" data-toggle="tooltip" data-placement="top" title="" data-original-title="&#x653E;&#x8FDB;&#x7B14;&#x8BB0;"></span></div></div><pre class="javascript hljs"><code class="javascript"><span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> endCount = <span class="hljs-number">0</span>;

<span class="hljs-function"><span class="hljs-keyword">function</span> <span class="hljs-title">onEnd</span>(<span class="hljs-params"></span>) </span>{
  <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (++endCount === <span class="hljs-number">2</span>) {
    pack.end();
  }
}

<span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> sourceStreamA = fstream.Reader({
    <span class="hljs-attr">type</span>: <span class="hljs-string">&quot;Directory&quot;</span>,
    <span class="hljs-attr">path</span>: sourceA
  })
  .on(<span class="hljs-string">&apos;end&apos;</span>, onEnd);

<span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> sourceStreamB = fstream.Reader({
    <span class="hljs-attr">type</span>: <span class="hljs-string">&quot;Directory&quot;</span>,
    <span class="hljs-attr">path</span>: sourceB
  })
  .on(<span class="hljs-string">&apos;end&apos;</span>, onEnd);</code></pre><p>&#x5728;&#x524D;&#x9762;&#x7684;&#x4EE3;&#x7801;&#x4E2D;&#xFF0C;&#x6211;&#x4EEC;&#x521B;&#x5EFA;&#x4E86;&#x4ECE;&#x4E24;&#x4E2A;&#x6E90;&#x76EE;&#x5F55;&#xFF08;<code>sourceStreamA</code>&#x548C;<code>sourceStreamB</code>&#xFF09;&#x4E2D;&#x8BFB;&#x53D6;&#x7684;<code>Stream</code>&#x90A3;&#x4E48;&#x5BF9;&#x4E8E;&#x6BCF;&#x4E2A;&#x6E90;<code>Stream</code>&#xFF0C;&#x6211;&#x4EEC;&#x9644;&#x52A0;&#x4E00;&#x4E2A;<code>end</code>&#x4E8B;&#x4EF6;&#x8BA2;&#x9605;&#x8005;&#xFF0C;&#x53EA;&#x6709;&#x5F53;&#x8FD9;&#x4E24;&#x4E2A;&#x76EE;&#x5F55;&#x88AB;&#x5B8C;&#x5168;&#x8BFB;&#x53D6;&#x65F6;&#xFF0C;&#x624D;&#x4F1A;&#x89E6;&#x53D1;<code>pack</code>&#x7684;<code>end</code>&#x4E8B;&#x4EF6;&#x3002;</p><p>&#x6700;&#x540E;&#xFF0C;&#x5408;&#x5E76;&#x4E24;&#x4E2A;<code>Stream</code>&#xFF1A;</p><div class="widget-codetool" style="display:none"><div class="widget-codetool--inner"><span class="selectCode code-tool" data-toggle="tooltip" data-placement="top" title="" data-original-title="&#x5168;&#x9009;"></span> <span type="button" class="copyCode code-tool" data-toggle="tooltip" data-placement="top" data-clipboard-text="sourceStreamA.pipe(pack, {end: false});

class="hljs-literal">false</span>});</code></pre><p>&#x6211;&#x4EEC;&#x5C06;&#x4E24;&#x4E2A;&#x6E90;&#x6587;&#x4EF6;&#x90FD;&#x538B;&#x7F29;&#x5230;<code>pack</code>&#x8FD9;&#x4E2A;<code>Stream</code>&#x4E2D;&#xFF0C;&#x5E76;&#x901A;&#x8FC7;&#x8BBE;&#x5B9A;<code>pipe()</code>&#x7684;<code>option</code>&#x53C2;&#x6570;&#x4E3A;<code>{end&#xFF1A;false}</code>&#x914D;&#x7F6E;&#x7EC8;&#x70B9;<code>Stream</code>&#x7684;&#x81EA;&#x52A8;&#x89E6;&#x53D1;<code>end</code>&#x4E8B;&#x4EF6;&#x3002;</p><p>&#x8FD9;&#x6837;&#xFF0C;&#x6211;&#x4EEC;&#x5DF2;&#x7ECF;&#x5B8C;&#x6210;&#x4E86;&#x6211;&#x4EEC;&#x7B80;&#x5355;&#x7684;<code>TAR</code>&#x7A0B;&#x5E8F;&#x3002;&#x6211;&#x4EEC;&#x53EF;&#x4EE5;&#x901A;&#x8FC7;&#x63D0;&#x4F9B;&#x76EE;&#x6807;&#x6587;&#x4EF6;&#x4F5C;&#x4E3A;&#x7B2C;&#x4E00;&#x4E2A;&#x547D;&#x4EE4;&#x884C;&#x53C2;&#x6570;&#xFF0C;&#x7136;&#x540E;&#x662F;&#x4E24;&#x4E2A;&#x6E90;&#x76EE;&#x5F55;&#x6765;&#x5C1D;&#x8BD5;&#x8FD0;&#x884C;&#x8FD9;&#x4E2A;&#x5B9E;&#x7528;&#x7A0B;&#x5E8F;&#xFF1A;</p><div   let totalChannels = sources.length;

  for(let i = 0; i &lt; sources.length; i++) {
    sources[i]
      .on(&apos;readable&apos;, function() { // [1]
        let chunk;
        while ((chunk = this.read()) !== null) {
          const outBuff = new Buffer(1 + 4 + chunk.length); // [2]
          outBuff.writeUInt8(i, 0);
          outBuff.writeUInt32BE(chunk.length, 1);
          chunk.copy(outBuff, 5);
          console.log(&apos;Sending packet to channel: &apos; + i);
          destination.write(outBuff); // [3]
        }
      })
      .on(&apos;end&apos;, () =&gt; { //[4]
        if (--totalChannels === 0) {
          destination.end();
        }
      });
  }
}" title="" data-original-title="&#x590D;&#x5236;"></span> <span type="button" class="saveToNote code-tool" data-toggle="tooltip" data-placement="top" title="" data-original-title="&#x653E;&#x8FDB;&#x7B14;&#x8BB0;"></span></div></div><pre class="javascript hljs"><code class="javascript"><span class="hljs-function"><span class="hljs-keyword">function</span> <span class="hljs-title">multiplexChannels</span>(<span class="hljs-params">sources, destination</span>) </span>{
  <span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> totalChannels = sources.length;

  <span class="hljs-keyword">for</span>(<span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> i = <span class="hljs-number">0</span>; i &lt; sources.length; i++) {
    sources[i]
      .on(<span class="hljs-string">&apos;readable&apos;</span>, <span class="hljs-function"><span class="hljs-keyword">function</span>(<span class="hljs-params"></span>) </span>{ <span class="hljs-comment">// [1]</span>
        <span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> chunk;
        <span class="hljs-keyword">while</span> ((chunk = <span class="hljs-keyword">this</span>.read()) !== <span class="hljs-literal">null</span>) {
          <span class="hljs-keyword">const</span> outBuff = <span class="hljs-keyword">new</span> Buffer(<span class="hljs-number">1</span> + <span class="hljs-number">4</span> + chunk.length); <span class="hljs-comment">// [2]</span>
          outBuff.writeUInt8(i, <span class="hljs-number">0</span>);
          outBuff.writeUInt32BE(chunk.length, <span class="hljs-number">1</span>);
          chunk.copy(outBuff, <span class="hljs-number">5</span>);
          <span class="hljs-built_in">console</span>.log(<span class="hljs-string">&apos;Sending packet to channel: &apos;</span> + i);
          destination.write(outBuff); <span class="hljs-comment">// [3]</span>
        }
      })
      .on(<span class="hljs-string">&apos;end&apos;</span>, () =&gt; { <span class="hljs-comment">//[4]</span>
        <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (--totalChannels === <span class="hljs-number">0</span>) {
          destination.end();
        }
      });
  }
}</code></pre><p><code>multiplexChannels()</code>&#x51FD;&#x6570;&#x63A5;&#x53D7;&#x8981;&#x590D;&#x7528;&#x7684;&#x6E90;<code>Stream</code>&#x4F5C;&#x4E3A;&#x8F93;&#x5165;<br>&#x548C;&#x590D;&#x7528;&#x63A5;&#x53E3;&#x4F5C;&#x4E3A;&#x53C2;&#x6570;&#xFF0C;&#x7136;&#x540E;&#x6267;&#x884C;&#x4EE5;&#x4E0B;&#x6B65;&#x9AA4;&#xFF1A;</p><ol><li>&#x5BF9;&#x4E8E;&#x6BCF;&#x4E2A;&#x6E90;<code>Stream</code>&#xFF0C;&#x5B83;&#x4F1A;&#x6CE8;&#x518C;&#x4E00;&#x4E2A;<code>readable</code>&#x4E8B;&#x4EF6;&#x4FA6;&#x542C;&#x5668;&#xFF0C;&#x6211;&#x4EEC;&#x4F7F;&#x7528;<code>non-flowing</code>&#x6A21;&#x5F0F;&#x4ECE;&#x6D41;&#x4E2D;&#x8BFB;&#x53D6;&#x6570;&#x636E;&#x3002;</li><li>&#x6BCF;&#x8BFB;&#x53D6;&#x4E00;&#x4E2A;&#x6570;&#x636E;&#x5757;&#xFF0C;&#x6211;&#x4EEC;&#x5C06;&#x5176;&#x5C01;&#x88C5;&#x5230;&#x4E00;&#x4E2A;&#x9996;&#x90E8;&#x4E2D;&#xFF0C;&#x9996;&#x90E8;&#x7684;&#x987A;&#x5E8F;&#x4E3A;&#xFF1A;<code>channel data-original-title="&#x5168;&#x9009;"></span> <span type="button" class="copyCode code-tool" data-toggle="tooltip" data-placement="top" data-clipboard-text="function demultiplexChannel(source, destinations) {
  let currentChannel = null;
  let currentLength = null;
  source
    .on(&apos;readable&apos;, () =&gt; { //[1]
      let chunk;
      if(currentChannel === null) {          //[2]
        chunk = source.read(1);
        currentChannel = chunk &amp;&amp; chunk.readUInt8(0);
      }
    
      if(currentLength === null) {          //[3]
        chunk = source.read(4);
        currentLength = chunk &amp;&amp; chunk.readUInt32BE(0);
        if(currentLength === null) {
          return;
        }
      }
    
      chunk = source.read(currentLength);        //[4]
      if(chunk === null) {
        return;
      }
    
      console.log(&apos;Received packet from: &apos; + currentChannel);
    
      destinations[currentChannel].write(chunk);      //[5]
      currentChannel = null;
      currentLength = null;
    })
    .on(&apos;end&apos;, () =&gt; {            //[6]
      destinations.forEach(destination =&gt; destination.end());
      console.log(&apos;Source channel closed&apos;);
    })
  ;
